# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# SLASH COMMANDS – MODERATION
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
@bot.tree.command(name="ban", description="Bannt einen Nutzer")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer", grund="Grund", delete_messages="Nachrichten löschen (Tage 0-7)")
@app_commands.default_permissions(ban_members=True)
async def slash_ban(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member,
                    grund: str = "Kein Grund angegeben", delete_messages: int = 0) -> None:
    ok, why = can_moderate(interaction.user, member, interaction.guild.me)
    if not ok:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Aktion blockiert", why, COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    pre_messages = await bot.db.aget_user_messages(interaction.guild.id, member.id)
    try:
        await member.ban(reason=f"{interaction.user}: {grund}", delete_message_days=min(max(delete_messages, 0), 7))
    except discord.Forbidden:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Forbidden", "Ich darf das nicht.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    case_id = await bot.db.acreate_case(interaction.guild.id, member.id, interaction.user.id, "ban", grund)
    if case_id and pre_messages:
        serializable = [{"channel_id": m.get("channel_id"), "content": m.get("content"),
                         "timestamp": m["timestamp"].isoformat() + "Z"} for m in pre_messages]
        await bot.db.aattach_messages_to_case(interaction.guild.id, case_id, serializable)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.BAN} Gebannt", f"{member.mention} wurde gebannt.", COLOR_DANGER,
                         [("Grund", grund, False), ("Case", f"#{case_id}", True),
                          ("Moderator", interaction.user.mention, True)])
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.BAN} Ban",
                         f"{member.mention} wurde gebannt von {interaction.user.mention}.",
                         COLOR_DANGER, [("Grund", grund, False), ("Case", f"#{case_id}", True)],
                         user=member, module="moderation")
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "ban", "moderation", f"Target: {member.id}, Grund: {grund}")


@bot.tree.command(name="kick", description="Kickt einen Nutzer")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer", grund="Grund")
@app_commands.default_permissions(kick_members=True)
async def slash_kick(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member,
                     grund: str = "Kein Grund angegeben") -> None:
    ok, why = can_moderate(interaction.user, member, interaction.guild.me)
    if not ok:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Aktion blockiert", why, COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    try:
        await member.kick(reason=f"{interaction.user}: {grund}")
    except discord.Forbidden:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Forbidden", "Ich darf das nicht.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    case_id = await bot.db.acreate_case(interaction.guild.id, member.id, interaction.user.id, "kick", grund)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.KICK} Gekickt", f"{member.mention} wurde gekickt.", COLOR_WARNING,
                         [("Grund", grund, False), ("Case", f"#{case_id}", True)])
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.KICK} Kick",
                         f"{member.mention} wurde gekickt von {interaction.user.mention}.",
                         COLOR_WARNING, [("Grund", grund, False)], user=member, module="moderation")
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "kick", "moderation", f"Target: {member.id}, Grund: {grund}")


@bot.tree.command(name="warn", description="Verwarnt einen Nutzer")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer", grund="Grund")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_messages=True)
async def slash_warn(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member,
                     grund: str = "Kein Grund angegeben") -> None:
    count = await bot.db.aadd_warning(interaction.guild.id, member.id, grund, interaction.user.id)
    case_id = await bot.db.acreate_case(interaction.guild.id, member.id, interaction.user.id, "warn", grund)
    await bot._check_warn_thresholds(member, count)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.WARN} Verwarnt", f"{member.mention} wurde verwarnt.", COLOR_WARNING,
                         [("Grund", grund, False), ("Verwarnungen gesamt", str(count), True),
                          ("Case", f"#{case_id}", True), ("Moderator", interaction.user.mention, True)])
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.WARN} Warn",
                         f"{member.mention} verwarnt von {interaction.user.mention}.",
                         COLOR_WARNING, [("Grund", grund, False), ("Total", str(count), True)],
                         user=member, module="moderation")


@bot.tree.command(name="mute", description="Versetzt einen Nutzer in Timeout")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer", dauer="Dauer (z.B. 10m, 2h, 1d)", grund="Grund")
@app_commands.default_permissions(moderate_members=True)
async def slash_mute(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member,
                     dauer: str = "60s", grund: str = "Kein Grund") -> None:
    ok, why = can_moderate(interaction.user, member, interaction.guild.me)
    if not ok:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Aktion blockiert", why, COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    seconds = parse_duration(dauer) or 60
    until = discord.utils.utcnow() + datetime.timedelta(seconds=seconds)
    try:
        await member.timeout(until, reason=f"{interaction.user}: {grund}")
    except discord.Forbidden:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Forbidden", "Ich darf das nicht.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    await bot.db.aadd_mute(interaction.guild.id, member.id, grund, interaction.user.id, seconds)
    case_id = await bot.db.acreate_case(interaction.guild.id, member.id, interaction.user.id, "timeout", grund, seconds)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.MUTE} Gemutet", f"{member.mention} wurde für **{_format_duration(seconds)}** gemutet.",
                         COLOR_WARNING, [("Grund", grund, False), ("Dauer", _format_duration(seconds), True),
                                         ("Case", f"#{case_id}", True)])
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.MUTE} Mute",
                         f"{member.mention} gemutet von {interaction.user.mention}",
                         COLOR_WARNING, [("Grund", grund, False), ("Dauer", _format_duration(seconds), True)],
                         user=member, module="moderation")


@bot.tree.command(name="unmute", description="Hebt den Timeout eines Nutzers auf")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer")
@app_commands.default_permissions(moderate_members=True)
async def slash_unmute(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member) -> None:
    try:
        await member.timeout(None, reason=f"Unmute durch {interaction.user}")
    except discord.Forbidden:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Forbidden", "Ich darf das nicht.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    await bot.db.adeactivate_mute(interaction.guild.id, member.id)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.UNMUTE} Entmutet", f"{member.mention} wurde entmutet.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.UNMUTE} Unmute",
                         f"{member.mention} entmutet von {interaction.user.mention}",
                         COLOR_SUCCESS, user=member, module="moderation")


@bot.tree.command(name="clear", description="Löscht Nachrichten im aktuellen Kanal")
@app_commands.describe(amount="Anzahl der Nachrichten (1-100)")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_messages=True)
async def slash_clear(interaction: discord.Interaction, amount: int = 10) -> None:
    amount = min(max(amount, 1), 100)
    await interaction.response.defer(ephemeral=True)
    try:
        deleted = await interaction.channel.purge(limit=amount)
    except discord.Forbidden:
        await interaction.followup.send(embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Forbidden", "Ich darf das nicht.", COLOR_DANGER))
        return
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.DELETE} Nachrichten gelöscht", f"**{len(deleted)}** Nachrichten gelöscht.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.DELETE} Clear",
                         f"{interaction.user.mention} hat {len(deleted)} Nachrichten in {interaction.channel.mention} gelöscht.",
                         COLOR_INFO, user=interaction.user, module="moderation")

@bot.tree.command(name="warnings", description="Zeigt die Verwarnungen eines Nutzers")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_messages=True)
async def slash_warnings(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member) -> None:
    warns = await bot.db.aget_warnings(interaction.guild.id, member.id)
    if not warns:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.CHANNEL} Verwarnungen",
                             f"{member.mention} hat keine Verwarnungen.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    else:
        cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
        expire_days = cfg.get("warn_system", {}).get("expire_days", 0)
        expire_info = f"\n*Verwarnungen verfallen nach {expire_days} Tagen.*" if expire_days > 0 else ""
        fields = []
        for i, w in enumerate(warns):
            ts = w.get("timestamp")
            ts_text = f"<t:{int(ts.timestamp())}:R>" if isinstance(ts, datetime.datetime) else str(ts)
            fields.append((f"#{i} – {w['reason'][:80]}", f"{ts_text} • Mod: <@{w.get('mod_id', '?')}>", False))
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.CHANNEL} Verwarnungen – {member.display_name}",
                             f"**{len(warns)}** Verwarnungen insgesamt.{expire_info}",
                             COLOR_WARNING, fields[:10], thumbnail=member.display_avatar.url)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)

@bot.tree.command(name="unban", description="Entbannt einen Nutzer")
@app_commands.describe(user_id="Nutzer-ID")
@app_commands.default_permissions(ban_members=True)
async def slash_unban(interaction: discord.Interaction, user_id: str) -> None:
    try:
        uid = int(user_id)
        user = await bot.fetch_user(uid)
        await interaction.guild.unban(user, reason=f"Unban durch {interaction.user}")
    except (discord.NotFound, ValueError):
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Nicht gefunden", "Nutzer/Ban nicht gefunden.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    except discord.Forbidden:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Forbidden", "Ich darf das nicht.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Entbannt", f"**{user}** wurde entbannt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.OK} Unban", f"{user} entbannt von {interaction.user.mention}",
                         COLOR_SUCCESS, module="moderation")

@bot.tree.command(name="voice_mute", description="Stummschaltet einen Nutzer in Voice-Kanälen")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer", dauer="Dauer (z.B. 10m, 1h, leer = dauerhaft)", grund="Grund")
@app_commands.default_permissions(mute_members=True)
async def slash_voice_mute(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member,
                            dauer: str = None, grund: str = "Kein Grund") -> None:
    ok, why = can_moderate(interaction.user, member, interaction.guild.me)
    if not ok:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Aktion blockiert", why, COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    seconds = parse_duration(dauer) if dauer else None
    # Sofort stummschalten wenn im Voice
    if member.voice and member.voice.channel:
        try:
            await member.edit(mute=True, reason=f"Voice-Mute durch {interaction.user}: {grund}")
        except (discord.Forbidden, discord.HTTPException):
            pass
    await bot.db.aadd_voice_mute(interaction.guild.id, member.id, interaction.user.id, grund, seconds)
    duration_str = _format_duration(seconds) if seconds else "Dauerhaft"
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.MUTE} Voice-Mute",
                         f"{member.mention} wurde im Voice stummgeschalten.",
                         COLOR_WARNING, [("Grund", grund, False), ("Dauer", duration_str, True)])
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.MUTE} Voice-Mute",
                         f"{member.mention} voice-gemutet von {interaction.user.mention} ({duration_str})",
                         COLOR_WARNING, user=member, module="voice_mod")
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "voice_mute", "voice_mod", f"Target: {member.id}, Dauer: {duration_str}")


@bot.tree.command(name="voice_unmute", description="Hebt die Voice-Stummschaltung auf")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer")
@app_commands.default_permissions(mute_members=True)
async def slash_voice_unmute(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member) -> None:
    if member.voice and member.voice.channel:
        try:
            await member.edit(mute=False, reason=f"Voice-Unmute durch {interaction.user}")
        except (discord.Forbidden, discord.HTTPException):
            pass
    await bot.db.adeactivate_voice_mute(interaction.guild.id, member.id)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.UNMUTE} Voice-Unmute",
                         f"{member.mention} wurde im Voice-Kanal entmutet.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.UNMUTE} Voice-Unmute",
                         f"{member.mention} voice-entmutet von {interaction.user.mention}",
                         COLOR_SUCCESS, user=member, module="voice_mod")

@note_group.command(name="add", description="Fügt eine interne Mod-Notiz zu einem Nutzer hinzu")

async def note_add(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member, notiz: str) -> None:

    embed = create_embed(f"{E.NOTE} Notiz hinzugefügt",

                         COLOR_INFO, thumbnail=member.display_avatar.url)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.NOTE} Mod-Notiz hinzugefügt",
                         f"**Nutzer:** {member.mention}\n**Von:** {interaction.user.mention}\n**Notiz:** {notiz[:300]}",
                         COLOR_INFO, user=interaction.user, module="notes")


@note_group.command(name="view", description="Zeigt alle Notizen zu einem Nutzer (nur Mods)")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_messages=True)
async def note_view(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member) -> None:
    notes = await bot.db.aget_mod_notes(interaction.guild.id, member.id)
    if not notes:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.NOTE} Notizen – {member.display_name}",
                             "Keine Notizen vorhanden.", COLOR_INFO)
    else:
        fields = []
        for i, n in enumerate(notes[:10]):
            ts = n.get("timestamp")
            ts_text = f"<t:{int(ts.timestamp())}:R>" if isinstance(ts, datetime.datetime) else str(ts)
            fields.append((f"#{i} – Mod: <@{n.get('mod_id', '?')}>",
                            f"{ts_text}\n{n.get('note', '')[:200]}", False))
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.NOTE} Notizen – {member.display_name}",
                             f"**{len(notes)}** Notiz(en).", COLOR_INFO, fields,
                             thumbnail=member.display_avatar.url)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)


@note_group.command(name="delete", description="Löscht eine Mod-Notiz (Index aus /note view)")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer", index="Index aus /note view")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_messages=True)
async def note_delete(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member, index: int) -> None:

    if ok:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Notiz gelöscht", f"Notiz #{index} von {member.mention} gelöscht.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    else:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Nicht gefunden", f"Index {index} existiert nicht.", COLOR_DANGER)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)

async def note_clear(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member) -> None:

    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# BACKUP-SYSTEM SLASH COMMANDS
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
backup_group = app_commands.Group(name="backup", description="Server-Backup verwalten")


async def _create_server_snapshot(guild: discord.Guild) -> dict:
    """Erstellt einen vollständigen Snapshot des Servers."""
    snapshot: Dict[str, Any] = {
        "name": guild.name,
        "icon_url": str(guild.icon.url) if guild.icon else None,
        "description": guild.description,
        "verification_level": guild.verification_level.value,
        "explicit_content_filter": guild.explicit_content_filter.value,
        "default_notifications": guild.default_notifications.value,
        "roles": [],
        "categories": [],
        "text_channels": [],
        "voice_channels": [],
        "created_at": datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
    }
    # Rollen (ohne @everyone)
    for role in guild.roles:
        if role.is_default():
            continue
        snapshot["roles"].append({
            "name": role.name,
            "color": role.color.value,
            "hoist": role.hoist,
            "mentionable": role.mentionable,
            "position": role.position,
            "permissions": role.permissions.value,
        })
    # Kategorien
    for cat in guild.categories:
        snapshot["categories"].append({
            "name": cat.name,
            "position": cat.position,
            "overwrites": {
                str(target.id): {
                    "type": "role" if isinstance(target, discord.Role) else "member",
                    "allow": overwrite.pair()[0].value,
                    "deny": overwrite.pair()[1].value,
                }
                for target, overwrite in cat.overwrites.items()
            },
        })
    # Text-Kanäle
    for ch in guild.text_channels:
        snapshot["text_channels"].append({
            "name": ch.name,
            "position": ch.position,
            "topic": ch.topic,
            "nsfw": ch.is_nsfw(),
            "slowmode_delay": ch.slowmode_delay,
            "category_name": ch.category.name if ch.category else None,
        })
    # Voice-Kanäle
    for vc in guild.voice_channels:
        snapshot["voice_channels"].append({
            "name": vc.name,
            "position": vc.position,
            "bitrate": vc.bitrate,
            "user_limit": vc.user_limit,
            "category_name": vc.category.name if vc.category else None,
        })
    return snapshot


@backup_group.command(name="create", description="Erstellt einen Server-Backup (Rollen, Kanäle, Farben, Rechte)")
@app_commands.describe(name="Optionaler Name für das Backup")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def backup_create(interaction: discord.Interaction, name: str = None) -> None:
    await interaction.response.defer(thinking=True)
    try:
        snapshot = await _create_server_snapshot(interaction.guild)
        if name:
            snapshot["label"] = name
        backup_id = await bot.db.acreate_backup(
            interaction.guild.id, interaction.guild.name,
            interaction.user.id, snapshot
        )
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.BACKUP} Backup erstellt",
                             f"Server-Backup wurde erfolgreich gespeichert!\n\n"
                             f"**Backup-ID:** `{backup_id}`\n"
                             f"**Name:** {name or 'Automatisch'}\n"
                             f"**Rollen:** {len(snapshot['roles'])}\n"
                             f"**Text-Kanäle:** {len(snapshot['text_channels'])}\n"
                             f"**Voice-Kanäle:** {len(snapshot['voice_channels'])}\n\n"
                             f"Verwende `/backup restore {backup_id}` zum Wiederherstellen (auch auf anderen Servern).",
                             COLOR_SUCCESS)
        await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed)
        await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.BACKUP} Backup erstellt",
                             f"{interaction.user.mention} hat ein Backup erstellt: `{backup_id}`",
                             COLOR_SUCCESS, user=interaction.user, module="backup")
        await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                       "backup_create", "backup_system", f"Backup-ID: {backup_id}")
    except Exception as e:
        await interaction.followup.send(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Backup fehlgeschlagen", f"Fehler: `{e}`", COLOR_DANGER))


@backup_group.command(name="restore", description="Stellt ein Backup wieder her (auch auf anderen Servern)")
@app_commands.describe(backup_id="Die Backup-ID", dry_run="Nur anzeigen, nicht wirklich wiederherstellen")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def backup_restore(interaction: discord.Interaction, backup_id: str, dry_run: bool = True) -> None:
    await interaction.response.defer(thinking=True)
    backup = await bot.db.aget_backup(backup_id)
    if not backup:
        await interaction.followup.send(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Backup nicht gefunden",
                               f"Kein Backup mit ID `{backup_id}` gefunden.", COLOR_DANGER))
        return
    data = backup.get("data", {})
    guild = interaction.guild
    log_lines = [
        f"**Backup-ID:** `{backup_id}`",
        f"**Original-Server:** {backup.get('guild_name', '?')}",
        f"**Erstellt:** {backup.get('created_at', '?')}",
        f"**Rollen:** {len(data.get('roles', []))}",
        f"**Text-Kanäle:** {len(data.get('text_channels', []))}",
        f"**Voice-Kanäle:** {len(data.get('voice_channels', []))}",
    ]
    if dry_run:
        log_lines.append("\n\n⚠️ **DRY-RUN** – Nichts wurde geändert. Setze `dry_run: Nein` um wirklich wiederherzustellen.")
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.BACKUP} Backup-Vorschau",
                             "\n".join(log_lines), COLOR_INFO)
        await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed)
        return
    # Echter Restore
    restored = {"roles": 0, "text_channels": 0, "voice_channels": 0, "errors": 0}
    existing_role_names = {r.name for r in guild.roles}
    for role_data in sorted(data.get("roles", []), key=lambda r: r.get("position", 0)):
        if role_data["name"] in existing_role_names:
            continue
        try:
            await rate_limited(
                guild.create_role,
                name=role_data["name"],
                color=discord.Color(role_data.get("color", 0)),
                hoist=role_data.get("hoist", False),
                mentionable=role_data.get("mentionable", False),
                permissions=discord.Permissions(role_data.get("permissions", 0)),
                reason=f"Backup-Restore {backup_id} durch {interaction.user}",
            )
            restored["roles"] += 1
        except Exception:
            restored["errors"] += 1
    existing_channel_names = {c.name for c in guild.channels}
    for ch_data in sorted(data.get("text_channels", []), key=lambda c: c.get("position", 0)):
        if ch_data["name"] in existing_channel_names:
            continue
        cat = None
        if ch_data.get("category_name"):
            cat = discord.utils.get(guild.categories, name=ch_data["category_name"])
        try:
            await rate_limited(
                guild.create_text_channel,
                ch_data["name"], category=cat,
                topic=ch_data.get("topic"),
                nsfw=ch_data.get("nsfw", False),
                slowmode_delay=ch_data.get("slowmode_delay", 0),
                reason=f"Backup-Restore {backup_id}",
            )
            restored["text_channels"] += 1
        except Exception:
            restored["errors"] += 1
    for vc_data in sorted(data.get("voice_channels", []), key=lambda c: c.get("position", 0)):
        if vc_data["name"] in existing_channel_names:
            continue
        cat = None
        if vc_data.get("category_name"):
            cat = discord.utils.get(guild.categories, name=vc_data["category_name"])
        try:
            await rate_limited(
                guild.create_voice_channel,
                vc_data["name"], category=cat,
                bitrate=min(vc_data.get("bitrate", 64000), guild.bitrate_limit),
                user_limit=vc_data.get("user_limit", 0),
                reason=f"Backup-Restore {backup_id}",
            )
            restored["voice_channels"] += 1
        except Exception:
            restored["errors"] += 1
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Backup wiederhergestellt",
                         f"**Backup-ID:** `{backup_id}`\n\n"
                         f"✅ **Rollen:** {restored['roles']} erstellt\n"
                         f"✅ **Text-Kanäle:** {restored['text_channels']} erstellt\n"
                         f"✅ **Voice-Kanäle:** {restored['voice_channels']} erstellt\n"
                         f"⚠️ **Fehler:** {restored['errors']}",
                         COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed)
    await bot.log_action(guild, f"{E.BACKUP} Backup wiederhergestellt",
                         f"{interaction.user.mention} hat Backup `{backup_id}` wiederhergestellt.",
                         COLOR_SUCCESS, user=interaction.user, module="backup")
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "backup_restore", "backup_system",
                                   f"Backup-ID: {backup_id}, Restored: {restored}")


@backup_group.command(name="list", description="Zeigt alle Backups dieses Servers")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def backup_list(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    backups = await bot.db.aget_guild_backups(interaction.guild.id)
    if not backups:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.BACKUP} Backups", "Keine Backups vorhanden.", COLOR_INFO)
        await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)
        return
    fields = []
    for b in backups[:10]:
        created = b.get("created_at")
        created_str = created.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M") if isinstance(created, datetime.datetime) else str(created)
        data = b.get("data", {})
        label = data.get("label", "Automatisch")
        fields.append((
            f"`{b['backup_id']}` – {label}",
            f"{created_str} • {len(data.get('roles', []))} Rollen, "
            f"{len(data.get('text_channels', []))} Kanäle",
            False
        ))
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.BACKUP} Backups – {interaction.guild.name}",
                         f"**{len(backups)}** Backup(s) vorhanden.", COLOR_INFO, fields)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)


@backup_group.command(name="delete", description="Löscht ein Backup")
@app_commands.describe(backup_id="Die Backup-ID")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def backup_delete(interaction: discord.Interaction, backup_id: str) -> None:
    ok = await bot.db.adelete_backup(backup_id)
    if ok:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Backup gelöscht", f"Backup `{backup_id}` wurde gelöscht.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    else:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Nicht gefunden", f"Kein Backup mit ID `{backup_id}`.", COLOR_DANGER)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)


bot.tree.add_command(backup_group)


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# WELCOME & AUTO-ROLE SLASH COMMANDS
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
welcome_group = app_commands.Group(name="welcome", description="Begrüßungssystem konfigurieren")


@welcome_group.command(name="set", description="Konfiguriert das Begrüßungssystem")
@app_commands.describe(
    channel="Kanal für Begrüßungsnachrichten",
    message="Nachrichtentext ({user} = Mention, {server} = Servername, {count} = Mitgliederzahl)",
    embed_title="Embed-Titel",
    embed_description="Embed-Beschreibung",
    image_url="URL für Embed-Bild",
    enabled="An/Aus"
)
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def welcome_set(interaction: discord.Interaction,
                       channel: discord.TextChannel = None,
                       message: str = None,
                       embed_title: str = None,
                       embed_description: str = None,
                       image_url: str = None,
                       enabled: bool = True) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    welcome_cfg = cfg.get("welcome_system", {})
    welcome_cfg["enabled"] = enabled
    if channel:
        welcome_cfg["channel_id"] = channel.id
    if message:
        welcome_cfg["message"] = message
    if embed_title:
        welcome_cfg["embed_title"] = embed_title
    if embed_description:
        welcome_cfg["embed_description"] = embed_description
    if image_url:
        welcome_cfg["embed_image_url"] = image_url
    cfg["welcome_system"] = welcome_cfg
    await bot.db.set_config(interaction.guild.id, cfg)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "welcome_set", "welcome_system", f"Kanal: {channel}, Enabled: {enabled}")
    ch_mention = channel.mention if channel else (f"<#{welcome_cfg.get('channel_id')}>" if welcome_cfg.get("channel_id") else "Nicht gesetzt")
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.WELCOME} Begrüßungssystem konfiguriert",
                         f"Status: {'✅ Aktiv' if enabled else '❌ Inaktiv'}\nKanal: {ch_mention}",
                         COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@welcome_group.command(name="test", description="Sendet eine Test-Begrüßungsnachricht für dich selbst")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def welcome_test(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    welcome_cfg = cfg.get("welcome_system", {})
    if not welcome_cfg.get("channel_id"):
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Kein Kanal konfiguriert",
                               "Nutze `/welcome set` um einen Kanal zu setzen.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    member = interaction.user
    guild = interaction.guild
    msg_text = welcome_cfg.get("message", "Willkommen auf {server}, {user}!")
    msg_text = msg_text.replace("{user}", member.mention).replace("{server}", guild.name).replace("{count}", str(guild.member_count))
    embed_title = welcome_cfg.get("embed_title", "Willkommen!")
    embed_desc = welcome_cfg.get("embed_description", "Schön, dass du da bist {user}!")
    embed_desc = embed_desc.replace("{user}", member.mention).replace("{server}", guild.name).replace("{count}", str(guild.member_count))
    embed_color = welcome_cfg.get("embed_color", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    welcome_embed = discord.Embed(title=embed_title, description=embed_desc, color=embed_color,
                                  timestamp=datetime.datetime.now(datetime.timezone.utc))
    welcome_embed.set_footer(text=FOOTER_TEXT, icon_url=FOOTER_ICON)
    if welcome_cfg.get("show_avatar"):
        welcome_embed.set_thumbnail(url=member.display_avatar.url)
    if welcome_cfg.get("embed_image_url"):
        welcome_embed.set_image(url=welcome_cfg["embed_image_url"])
    channel = guild.get_channel(welcome_cfg["channel_id"])
    if channel:
        await channel.send(content=f"[TEST] {msg_text}", embed=welcome_embed)
    await interaction.response.send_message(f"{E.OK} Test-Begrüßung in {channel.mention if channel else 'unbekannt'} gesendet!", ephemeral=True)


bot.tree.add_command(welcome_group)


autorole_group = app_commands.Group(name="autorole", description="Auto-Rollen beim Join konfigurieren")


@autorole_group.command(name="add", description="Fügt eine Auto-Rolle hinzu")
@app_commands.describe(role="Rolle", bot_role="Nur für Bots?")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def autorole_add(interaction: discord.Interaction, role: discord.Role, bot_role: bool = False) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    auto_cfg = cfg.get("auto_role", {})
    auto_cfg["enabled"] = True
    key = "bot_roles" if bot_role else "roles"
    role_list = auto_cfg.get(key, [])
    if role.id not in role_list:
        role_list.append(role.id)
    auto_cfg[key] = role_list
    cfg["auto_role"] = auto_cfg
    await bot.db.set_config(interaction.guild.id, cfg)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "autorole_add", "auto_role", f"Rolle: {role.id}, Bot: {bot_role}")
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.ROLE_ADD} Auto-Rolle hinzugefügt",
                         f"{role.mention} wird beim Join {'von Bots' if bot_role else 'von Nutzern'} vergeben.",
                         COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@autorole_group.command(name="remove", description="Entfernt eine Auto-Rolle")
@app_commands.describe(role="Rolle", bot_role="Bot-Rolle?")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def autorole_remove(interaction: discord.Interaction, role: discord.Role, bot_role: bool = False) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    auto_cfg = cfg.get("auto_role", {})
    key = "bot_roles" if bot_role else "roles"
    role_list = auto_cfg.get(key, [])
    if role.id in role_list:
        role_list.remove(role.id)
    auto_cfg[key] = role_list
    cfg["auto_role"] = auto_cfg
    await bot.db.set_config(interaction.guild.id, cfg)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.ROLE_DEL} Auto-Rolle entfernt",
                         f"{role.mention} wurde aus den Auto-Rollen entfernt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@autorole_group.command(name="list", description="Zeigt alle konfigurierten Auto-Rollen")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def autorole_list(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    auto_cfg = cfg.get("auto_role", {})
    roles_str = " ".join(f"<@&{rid}>" for rid in auto_cfg.get("roles", [])) or "Keine"
    bot_roles_str = " ".join(f"<@&{rid}>" for rid in auto_cfg.get("bot_roles", [])) or "Keine"
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.ROLE} Auto-Rollen",
                         f"Status: {'✅ Aktiv' if auto_cfg.get('enabled') else '❌ Inaktiv'}",
                         COLOR_INFO,
                         [("Nutzer-Rollen", roles_str, False), ("Bot-Rollen", bot_roles_str, False)])
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)


@autorole_group.command(name="toggle", description="Aktiviert/Deaktiviert Auto-Rollen")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def autorole_toggle(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    auto_cfg = cfg.get("auto_role", {})
    auto_cfg["enabled"] = not auto_cfg.get("enabled", False)
    cfg["auto_role"] = auto_cfg
    await bot.db.set_config(interaction.guild.id, cfg)
    status = "✅ Aktiviert" if auto_cfg["enabled"] else "❌ Deaktiviert"
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.ROLE} Auto-Rollen {status}", "", COLOR_SUCCESS if auto_cfg["enabled"] else COLOR_WARNING)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


bot.tree.add_command(autorole_group)


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# GDPR / DSGVO SLASH COMMAND
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
@bot.tree.command(name="gdpr", description="Löscht alle Daten eines Nutzers (DSGVO-Löschanfrage)")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer (leer = dich selbst)", server_only="Nur Daten dieses Servers löschen")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_gdpr(interaction: discord.Interaction,
                     member: discord.Member = None,
                     server_only: bool = True) -> None:
    if member and not interaction.user.guild_permissions.administrator:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Keine Berechtigung",
                               "Nur Administratoren können Daten anderer Nutzer löschen.", COLOR_DANGER),
            ephemeral=True)
        return
    target = member or interaction.user
    guild_id = interaction.guild.id if server_only else None
    await interaction.response.defer(thinking=True, ephemeral=True)
    deleted = await bot.db.adelete_user_data(target.id, guild_id)
    req_id = await bot.db.aadd_gdpr_request(target.id, guild_id, "admin_delete")
    total = sum(deleted.values())
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.GDPR} DSGVO-Löschung abgeschlossen",
                         f"**{total}** Datensätze für {target.mention} gelöscht.\n"
                         f"Anfrage-ID: `{req_id}`\n\n" +
                         "\n".join(f"• {k}: {v}" for k, v in deleted.items()),
                         COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.GDPR} DSGVO-Löschung",
                         f"{interaction.user.mention} hat Daten von {target.mention} gelöscht.\n"
                         f"Anfrage-ID: `{req_id}`",
                         COLOR_INFO, user=interaction.user, module="gdpr")
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "gdpr_delete", "gdpr", f"Target: {target.id}, ReqID: {req_id}")


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# ADMIN-AUDIT LOG COMMAND
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
@bot.tree.command(name="admin-audit", description="Zeigt die Admin-Aktionen-Log dieses Servers")
@app_commands.describe(limit="Anzahl der Einträge (max 25)")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_admin_audit(interaction: discord.Interaction, limit: int = 20) -> None:
    limit = min(max(limit, 1), 25)
    audits = await bot.db.aget_admin_audits(interaction.guild.id, limit)
    if not audits:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.AUDIT_LOG} Admin-Audit-Log", "Keine Einträge vorhanden.", COLOR_INFO)
        await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)
        return
    fields = []
    for a in audits:
        ts = a.get("timestamp")
        ts_text = f"<t:{int(ts.timestamp())}:R>" if isinstance(ts, datetime.datetime) else str(ts)
        fields.append((
            f"{a.get('action', '?')} – {a.get('module', '?')}",
            f"{ts_text} • Admin: <@{a.get('admin_id', '?')}>\n{a.get('details', '')[:150]}",
            False
        ))
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.AUDIT_LOG} Admin-Audit-Log – {interaction.guild.name}",
                         f"Letzte **{len(audits)}** Admin-Aktionen.", COLOR_INFO, fields[:10])
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# WARN-EXPIRE SLASH COMMAND
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
@bot.tree.command(name="warn_expire", description="Setzt die Verfallszeit für Verwarnungen")
@app_commands.describe(tage="Tage bis Verwarnungen verfallen (0 = nie verfallen)")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_warn_expire(interaction: discord.Interaction, tage: int) -> None:
    if tage < 0:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Ungültig", "Tage müssen >= 0 sein.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    warn_cfg = cfg.get("warn_system", {})
    warn_cfg["expire_days"] = tage
    cfg["warn_system"] = warn_cfg
    await bot.db.set_config(interaction.guild.id, cfg)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "warn_expire_set", "warn_system", f"Expire Days: {tage}")
    msg = f"Verwarnungen verfallen jetzt nach **{tage} Tagen**." if tage > 0 else "Verwarnungen verfallen **nie**."
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.WARN} Warn-Verfall konfiguriert", msg, COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# SECURITY GROUP
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
security_group = app_commands.Group(name="security", description="Security-Einstellungen verwalten")


@security_group.command(name="view", description="Zeigt die aktuelle Security-Konfiguration")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def security_view(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    modules = ["anti_spam", "anti_nuke", "anti_raid", "anti_mention", "automod",
               "anti_ghost_ping", "anti_scam", "anti_url_shortener", "voice_mod"]
    fields = []
    for mod in modules:
        mod_cfg = cfg.get(mod, {})
        status = f"{E.OK} Aktiv" if mod_cfg.get("enabled") else f"{E.FAIL} Inaktiv"
        fields.append((mod.replace("_", " ").title(), status, True))
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.SHIELD} Security Übersicht",
                         f"Aktuelle Konfiguration für **{interaction.guild.name}**",
                         COLOR_PRIMARY, fields,
                         thumbnail=interaction.guild.icon.url if interaction.guild.icon else None)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@security_group.command(name="toggle", description="Aktiviert/Deaktiviert ein Modul")
@app_commands.describe(module="Modul-Name (z.B. anti_spam)")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def security_toggle(interaction: discord.Interaction, module: str) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    if module not in cfg or not isinstance(cfg[module], dict):
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Fehler", f"Modul `{module}` nicht gefunden.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    current = cfg[module].get("enabled", False)
    await bot.db.update_module(interaction.guild.id, module, "enabled", not current)
    status = f"{E.OK} Aktiviert" if not current else f"{E.FAIL} Deaktiviert"
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.SETTINGS} Modul geändert", f"**{module}** wurde **{status}**.",
                         COLOR_SUCCESS if not current else COLOR_WARNING)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   f"toggle_{module}", module, f"Enabled: {not current}")


@security_group.command(name="set", description="Setzt einen Wert in einem Modul")
@app_commands.describe(module="Modul", setting="Einstellung", value="Wert")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def security_set(interaction: discord.Interaction, module: str, setting: str, value: str) -> None:
    parsed: Any = value
    if value.lower() in ("true", "false"):
        parsed = value.lower() == "true"
    elif value.isdigit():
        parsed = int(value)
    await bot.db.update_module(interaction.guild.id, module, setting, parsed)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Einstellung gespeichert", f"`{module}.{setting}` = `{parsed}`", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   f"set_{module}_{setting}", module, f"Value: {parsed}")


@security_group.command(name="punishment", description="Setzt die Strafe für ein Modul")
@app_commands.describe(module="Modul", punishment_type="warn / timeout / kick / ban")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def security_punishment(interaction: discord.Interaction, module: str, punishment_type: str) -> None:
    if punishment_type not in VALID_PUNISHMENTS:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Ungültige Strafe",
                               f"Erlaubte Werte: {', '.join(VALID_PUNISHMENTS)}", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    await bot.db.update_module(interaction.guild.id, module, "punishment", punishment_type)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Strafe gesetzt",
                         f"Strafe für **{module}** auf **{punishment_type}** gesetzt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   f"punishment_{module}", module, f"Punishment: {punishment_type}")


@security_group.command(name="reset", description="Setzt ein Modul auf Standardwerte zurück")
@app_commands.describe(module="Modul-Name")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def security_reset(interaction: discord.Interaction, module: str) -> None:
    if module not in DEFAULT_CONFIG:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Fehler", f"Modul `{module}` nicht gefunden.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    default_val = DEFAULT_CONFIG[module]
    cfg[module] = default_val.copy() if isinstance(default_val, (dict, list)) else default_val
    await bot.db.set_config(interaction.guild.id, cfg)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.DUP} Modul zurückgesetzt",
                         f"**{module}** wurde auf Standardwerte zurückgesetzt.", COLOR_INFO)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   f"reset_{module}", module, "Reset to defaults")


bot.tree.add_command(security_group)


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# WHITELIST GROUP
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
whitelist_group = app_commands.Group(name="whitelist", description="Whitelist verwalten")

WL_CATEGORIES = [
    app_commands.Choice(name="Nutzer", value="users"),
    app_commands.Choice(name="Rollen", value="roles"),
    app_commands.Choice(name="Kanäle", value="channels"),
    app_commands.Choice(name="Bypass Anti-Spam", value="bypass_antispam"),
    app_commands.Choice(name="Bypass Anti-Nuke", value="bypass_antinuke"),
]


@whitelist_group.command(name="add", description="Fügt einen Eintrag zur Whitelist hinzu")
@app_commands.describe(category="Kategorie wählen", entry_id="ID des Eintrags")
@app_commands.choices(category=WL_CATEGORIES)
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def whitelist_add(interaction: discord.Interaction,
                        category: app_commands.Choice[str], entry_id: str) -> None:
    if not entry_id.isdigit():
        await interaction.response.send_message(f"{E.FAIL} Die ID muss eine Zahl sein.", ephemeral=True)
        return
    await bot.db.aadd_whitelist(interaction.guild.id, category.value, int(entry_id))
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Whitelist aktualisiert",
                         f"ID `{entry_id}` zur Kategorie **{category.name}** hinzugefügt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@whitelist_group.command(name="bulk_add", description="Fügt viele IDs gleichzeitig hinzu")
@app_commands.describe(category="Kategorie wählen", ids="IDs getrennt durch Komma oder Leerzeichen")
@app_commands.choices(category=WL_CATEGORIES)
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def whitelist_bulk_add(interaction: discord.Interaction,
                             category: app_commands.Choice[str], ids: str) -> None:
    id_list = re.split(r'[,\s]+', ids.strip())
    added = 0
    for eid in id_list:
        if eid.isdigit():
            await bot.db.aadd_whitelist(interaction.guild.id, category.value, int(eid))
            added += 1
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Bulk-Add abgeschlossen",
                         f"**{added}** IDs wurden zur Kategorie **{category.name}** hinzugefügt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@whitelist_group.command(name="remove", description="Entfernt einen Eintrag aus der Whitelist")
@app_commands.describe(category="Kategorie", entry_id="ID")
@app_commands.choices(category=WL_CATEGORIES)
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def whitelist_remove(interaction: discord.Interaction,
                           category: app_commands.Choice[str], entry_id: str) -> None:
    if not entry_id.isdigit():
        await interaction.response.send_message(f"{E.FAIL} Die ID muss eine Zahl sein.", ephemeral=True)
        return
    await bot.db.aremove_whitelist(interaction.guild.id, category.value, int(entry_id))
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Entfernt", f"ID `{entry_id}` aus **{category.name}** entfernt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@whitelist_group.command(name="add_user", description="Fügt einen Nutzer bequem zur Whitelist hinzu")
@app_commands.describe(user="Nutzer")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def whitelist_add_user(interaction: discord.Interaction, user: discord.User) -> None:
    await bot.db.aadd_whitelist(interaction.guild.id, "users", user.id)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Nutzer hinzugefügt",
                         f"{user.mention} wurde zur Whitelist hinzugefügt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@whitelist_group.command(name="add_role", description="Fügt eine Rolle bequem zur Whitelist hinzu")
@app_commands.describe(role="Rolle")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def whitelist_add_role(interaction: discord.Interaction, role: discord.Role) -> None:
    await bot.db.aadd_whitelist(interaction.guild.id, "roles", role.id)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Rolle hinzugefügt",
                         f"{role.mention} wurde zur Whitelist hinzugefügt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@whitelist_group.command(name="add_channel", description="Fügt einen Kanal bequem zur Whitelist hinzu")
@app_commands.describe(channel="Kanal")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def whitelist_add_channel(interaction: discord.Interaction, channel: discord.TextChannel) -> None:
    await bot.db.aadd_whitelist(interaction.guild.id, "channels", channel.id)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Kanal hinzugefügt",
                         f"{channel.mention} wurde zur Whitelist hinzugefügt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@whitelist_group.command(name="remove_role", description="Entfernt eine Rolle bequem aus der Whitelist")
@app_commands.describe(role="Rolle")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def whitelist_remove_role(interaction: discord.Interaction, role: discord.Role) -> None:
    await bot.db.aremove_whitelist(interaction.guild.id, "roles", role.id)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Rolle entfernt",
                         f"{role.mention} wurde aus der Whitelist entfernt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@whitelist_group.command(name="clear", description="Leert eine Whitelist-Kategorie komplett")
@app_commands.describe(category="Kategorie")
@app_commands.choices(category=WL_CATEGORIES)
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def whitelist_clear(interaction: discord.Interaction, category: app_commands.Choice[str]) -> None:
    wl = bot.db.get_whitelist(interaction.guild.id)
    wl[category.value] = []
    await bot.db.set_whitelist(interaction.guild.id, wl)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Geleert",
                         f"Kategorie **{category.name}** wurde komplett geleert.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@whitelist_group.command(name="list", description="Zeigt die aktuelle Whitelist")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def whitelist_list(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    wl = bot.db.get_whitelist(interaction.guild.id)
    fields = [
        (f"{E.USERS} Nutzer", "\n".join(f"<@{uid}>" for uid in wl.get("users", [])) or "Keine", False),
        (f"{E.ROLES} Rollen", "\n".join(f"<@&{rid}>" for rid in wl.get("roles", [])) or "Keine", False),
        (f"{E.CHANNELS} Kanäle", "\n".join(f"<#{cid}>" for cid in wl.get("channels", [])) or "Keine", False),
        (f"{E.SPAM} Bypass Anti-Spam", "\n".join(f"<@{uid}>" for uid in wl.get("bypass_antispam", [])) or "Keine", False),
        (f"{E.NUKE} Bypass Anti-Nuke", "\n".join(f"<@{uid}>" for uid in wl.get("bypass_antinuke", [])) or "Keine", False),
    ]
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.CHANNEL} Whitelist", f"Whitelist für **{interaction.guild.name}**", COLOR_INFO, fields)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


bot.tree.add_command(whitelist_group)


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# AUTOMOD GROUP
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
automod_group = app_commands.Group(name="automod", description="AutoMod verwalten")


@automod_group.command(name="badword_add", description="Fügt ein verbotenes Wort hinzu")
@app_commands.describe(word="Das verbotene Wort")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_guild=True)
async def automod_badword_add(interaction: discord.Interaction, word: str) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    bad_words = cfg.get("automod", {}).get("bad_words", [])
    if word.lower() not in bad_words:
        bad_words.append(word.lower())
        await bot.db.update_module(interaction.guild.id, "automod", "bad_words", bad_words)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Wort hinzugefügt", f"`{word}` zur Wortliste hinzugefügt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "badword_add", "automod", f"Word: {word}")


@automod_group.command(name="badword_remove", description="Entfernt ein verbotenes Wort")
@app_commands.describe(word="Das Wort")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_guild=True)
async def automod_badword_remove(interaction: discord.Interaction, word: str) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    bad_words = cfg.get("automod", {}).get("bad_words", [])
    bad_words = [w for w in bad_words if w != word.lower()]
    await bot.db.update_module(interaction.guild.id, "automod", "bad_words", bad_words)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Wort entfernt", f"`{word}` aus der Wortliste entfernt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@automod_group.command(name="badword_list", description="Zeigt alle verbotenen Wörter")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_guild=True)
async def automod_badword_list(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    bad_words = cfg.get("automod", {}).get("bad_words", [])
    if not bad_words:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.CHANNEL} Verbotene Wörter", "Keine verbotenen Wörter konfiguriert.", COLOR_INFO)
    else:
        word_list = "\n".join(f"• ||{w}||" for w in bad_words)
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.CHANNEL} Verbotene Wörter",
                             f"**{len(bad_words)}** verbotene Wörter:\n{word_list}", COLOR_WARNING)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)


@automod_group.command(name="regex_add", description="Fügt eine Custom Regex-Regel hinzu")
@app_commands.describe(pattern="Regex-Pattern (Python re)")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_guild=True)
async def automod_regex_add(interaction: discord.Interaction, pattern: str) -> None:
    try:
        re.compile(pattern)
    except re.error as ex:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Ungültiges Regex", f"`{ex}`", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    rules = cfg.get("automod", {}).get("regex_rules", [])
    rules.append(pattern)
    await bot.db.update_module(interaction.guild.id, "automod", "regex_rules", rules)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Regex hinzugefügt", f"Regel hinzugefügt:\n`{pattern[:200]}`", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@automod_group.command(name="regex_remove", description="Entfernt eine Regex-Regel per Index")
@app_commands.describe(index="Index aus /automod regex_list")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_guild=True)
async def automod_regex_remove(interaction: discord.Interaction, index: int) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    rules = cfg.get("automod", {}).get("regex_rules", [])
    if not (0 <= index < len(rules)):
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Ungültig", f"Index {index} existiert nicht.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    removed = rules.pop(index)
    await bot.db.update_module(interaction.guild.id, "automod", "regex_rules", rules)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Regex entfernt", f"Entfernt: `{removed[:200]}`", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@automod_group.command(name="regex_list", description="Zeigt alle Custom Regex-Regeln")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_guild=True)
async def automod_regex_list(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    rules = cfg.get("automod", {}).get("regex_rules", [])
    if not rules:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.CHANNEL} Regex-Regeln", "Keine Custom-Regeln konfiguriert.", COLOR_INFO)
    else:
        fields = [(f"#{i}", f"`{p[:200]}`", False) for i, p in enumerate(rules)]
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.CHANNEL} Regex-Regeln", f"**{len(rules)}** Regeln aktiv.", COLOR_WARNING, fields)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)


@automod_group.command(name="domain_allow", description="Erlaubt eine Domain im Link-Filter")
@app_commands.describe(domain="Domain (z.B. youtube.com)")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_guild=True)
async def automod_domain_allow(interaction: discord.Interaction, domain: str) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    allowed = cfg.get("automod", {}).get("allowed_domains", [])
    if domain.lower() not in allowed:
        allowed.append(domain.lower())
        await bot.db.update_module(interaction.guild.id, "automod", "allowed_domains", allowed)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Domain erlaubt", f"`{domain}` zur Whitelist hinzugefügt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


bot.tree.add_command(automod_group)

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# CASE-SYSTEM SLASH COMMANDS
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
@bot.tree.command(name="case", description="Zeigt einen Case (Mod-Vorgang) per ID an")
@app_commands.describe(case_id="Die Case-ID (z. B. 42)")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_messages=True)
async def slash_case(interaction: discord.Interaction, case_id: int) -> None:
    case = await bot.db.aget_case(interaction.guild.id, case_id)
    if not case:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.NO} Case nicht gefunden",
                               f"Es gibt keinen Case mit ID `{case_id}` in diesem Server.", COLOR_DANGER),
            ephemeral=True)
        return
    try:
        user = interaction.guild.get_member(case["user_id"]) or await bot.fetch_user(case["user_id"])
        mod = interaction.guild.get_member(case["mod_id"]) or await bot.fetch_user(case["mod_id"])
    except Exception:
        user = None
        mod = None
    user_name = f"{user} (`{case['user_id']}`)" if user else f"`{case['user_id']}`"
    mod_name = f"{mod}" if mod else f"`{case['mod_id']}`"
    arch_count = len(case.get("message_archive", []))
    ev_count = len(case.get("evidence", []))
    history = case.get("reason_history", [])
    fields = [
        (f"{E.USER} User", user_name, True),
        (f"{E.MOD} Moderator", mod_name, True),
        (f"{E.WARN} Aktion", case["action"].upper(), True),
        (f"{E.CLOCK} Dauer", _format_duration(case.get("duration")), True),
        (f"{E.MESSAGE} Archiv-Nachrichten", str(arch_count), True),
        (f"{E.IMAGE} Beweise", str(ev_count), True),
        (f"{E.NOTE} Grund", case.get("reason", "—")[:1000], False),
    ]
    if history:
        last = history[-1]
        fields.append((f"{E.EDIT} Letzte Grund-Änderung",
                        f"<t:{int(last['changed_at'].timestamp())}:R> von <@{last['changed_by']}>", False))
    if case.get("evidence"):
        ev_lines = [f"`{i}` [Link]({ev['url']})" + (f" – {ev.get('note', '')}" if ev.get("note") else "")
                    for i, ev in enumerate(case["evidence"][:5], 1)]
        fields.append((f"{E.IMAGE} Beweise (max. 5)", "\n".join(ev_lines), False))
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.SHIELD} Case #{case_id}",
                         f"Erstellt <t:{int(case['created_at'].timestamp())}:F>",
                         COLOR_INFO if case["action"] != "ban" else COLOR_DANGER, fields,
                         thumbnail=user.display_avatar.url if isinstance(user, (discord.Member, discord.User)) else None)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


# /case search – Alle Cases eines Nutzers
@bot.tree.command(name="case_search", description="Sucht alle Cases eines Nutzers")
@app_commands.describe(member="Nutzer", limit="Maximale Anzahl (Standard: 20)")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_messages=True)
async def slash_case_search(interaction: discord.Interaction, member: discord.Member, limit: int = 20) -> None:
    await interaction.response.defer(thinking=True)
    limit = min(max(limit, 1), 50)
    cases = await bot.db.aget_user_cases(interaction.guild.id, member.id, limit)
    if not cases:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.NOTE} Keine Cases gefunden",
                             f"Keine Cases für {member.mention} auf diesem Server.", COLOR_INFO)
        await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)
        return
    fields = []
    for c in cases[:10]:
        ts = c.get("created_at")
        ts_text = f"<t:{int(ts.timestamp())}:R>" if isinstance(ts, datetime.datetime) else "?"
        action_emoji = {"ban": E.BAN, "kick": E.KICK, "warn": E.WARN, "timeout": E.MUTE}.get(c.get("action", ""), E.NOTE)
        fields.append((f"{action_emoji} Case #{c['case_id']} – {c.get('action', '?').upper()}",
                        f"{ts_text} • Mod: <@{c.get('mod_id', '?')}>\n{c.get('reason', '—')[:100]}", False))
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.SHIELD} Cases – {member.display_name}",
                         f"**{len(cases)}** Case(s) gefunden.", COLOR_INFO, fields,
                         thumbnail=member.display_avatar.url)
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)


# /case export – Cases als CSV/JSON
@bot.tree.command(name="case_export", description="Exportiert alle Cases dieses Servers als CSV oder JSON")
@app_commands.describe(format="csv oder json", member="Optional: nur Cases dieses Nutzers")
@app_commands.choices(format=[app_commands.Choice(name="CSV", value="csv"),
                               app_commands.Choice(name="JSON", value="json")])
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_case_export(interaction: discord.Interaction,
                             format: app_commands.Choice[str],
                             member: discord.Member = None) -> None:
    await interaction.response.defer(thinking=True, ephemeral=True)
    if member:
        cases = await bot.db.aget_user_cases(interaction.guild.id, member.id, 500)
    else:
        cases = await bot.db.aget_recent_cases(interaction.guild.id, 500)

    if not cases:
        await interaction.followup.send(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Keine Cases", "Keine Cases gefunden.", COLOR_INFO), ephemeral=True)
        return

    if format.value == "csv":
        output = StringIO()
        writer = csv.writer(output)
        writer.writerow(["case_id", "user_id", "mod_id", "action", "reason", "duration", "created_at"])
        for c in cases:
            created = c.get("created_at", "")
            if isinstance(created, datetime.datetime):
                created = created.isoformat()
            writer.writerow([c.get("case_id"), c.get("user_id"), c.get("mod_id"), c.get("action"),
                              c.get("reason", "")[:200], c.get("duration", ""), created])
        file_content = output.getvalue().encode("utf-8")
        filename = f"cases_{interaction.guild.id}.csv"
    else:
        export_data = []
        for c in cases:
            created = c.get("created_at", "")
            if isinstance(created, datetime.datetime):
                created = created.isoformat()
            export_data.append({
                "case_id": c.get("case_id"), "user_id": c.get("user_id"),
                "mod_id": c.get("mod_id"), "action": c.get("action"),
                "reason": c.get("reason", ""), "duration": c.get("duration"),
                "created_at": created,
            })
        file_content = json.dumps(export_data, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2).encode("utf-8")
        filename = f"cases_{interaction.guild.id}.json"

    file = discord.File(io.BytesIO(file_content), filename=filename)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Cases exportiert",
                         f"**{len(cases)}** Cases wurden als {format.name} exportiert.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed, file=file, ephemeral=True)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "case_export", "cases", f"Format: {format.value}, Count: {len(cases)}")


@bot.tree.command(name="reason", description="Ändert/ergänzt den Grund eines Cases")
@app_commands.describe(case_id="Die Case-ID", grund="Der neue oder ergänzende Grund")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_messages=True)
async def slash_reason(interaction: discord.Interaction, case_id: int, grund: str) -> None:
    ok = await bot.db.aupdate_case_reason(interaction.guild.id, case_id, grund, interaction.user.id)
    if not ok:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.NO} Case nicht gefunden",
                               f"Kein Case `{case_id}` in diesem Server.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    ACTIVITY.push("case", f"Case #{case_id} – Grund aktualisiert von {interaction.user}.",
                  guild_id=interaction.guild.id, guild_name=interaction.guild.name)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.EDIT} Case #{case_id} – Grund geändert",
                         f"**Geändert von:** {interaction.user.mention}\n**Neuer Grund:** {grund[:1000]}",
                         COLOR_INFO, user=interaction.user, module="cases")
    await interaction.response.send_message(
        embed=create_embed(f"{E.OK} Case #{case_id} aktualisiert",
                           f"Neuer Grund:\n```\n{grund[:500]}\n```", COLOR_SUCCESS), ephemeral=True)


@bot.tree.command(name="addproof", description="Fügt einem Case einen Beweis (URL/Screenshot) hinzu")
@app_commands.describe(case_id="Die Case-ID", proof="Ein Bild-Anhang als Beweis",
                       url="ODER eine direkte URL zum Beweis", notiz="Optionale Notiz zum Beweis")
@app_commands.default_permissions(manage_messages=True)
async def slash_addproof(interaction: discord.Interaction, case_id: int,
                          proof: Optional[discord.Attachment] = None,
                          url: Optional[str] = None, notiz: Optional[str] = None) -> None:
    if not proof and not url:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.NO} Fehlender Beweis",
                               "Hänge ein Bild **oder** gib eine URL an.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    final_url = proof.url if proof else url
    ok = await bot.db.aadd_case_evidence(interaction.guild.id, case_id, final_url, interaction.user.id, notiz or "")
    if not ok:
        await interaction.response.send_message(
            embed=create_embed(f"{E.NO} Case nicht gefunden",
                               f"Kein Case `{case_id}` in diesem Server.", COLOR_DANGER), ephemeral=True)
        return
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.IMAGE} Case #{case_id} – Beweis hinzugefügt",
                         f"**Von:** {interaction.user.mention}\n[Beweis-Link]({final_url})\n"
                         f"{('**Notiz:** ' + notiz) if notiz else ''}",
                         COLOR_INFO, user=interaction.user, module="cases")
    await interaction.response.send_message(
        embed=create_embed(f"{E.OK} Beweis gespeichert",
                           f"Case #{case_id} hat jetzt einen neuen Beweis.", COLOR_SUCCESS), ephemeral=True)


@bot.tree.command(name="setarchive", description="Aktiviert/deaktiviert das 48h-Nachrichten-Archiv")
@app_commands.describe(enabled="An/Aus")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_setarchive(interaction: discord.Interaction, enabled: bool) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    arch = cfg.get("message_archive", {}) or {}
    arch["enabled"] = bool(enabled)
    arch.setdefault("ttl_hours", 48)
    cfg["message_archive"] = arch
    await bot.db.set_config(interaction.guild.id, cfg)
    state = "AKTIVIERT ✅" if enabled else "DEAKTIVIERT ❌"
    await interaction.response.send_message(
        embed=create_embed(f"{E.SHIELD} Nachrichten-Archiv {state}",
                           ("Ab sofort werden alle User-Nachrichten **48 Stunden** in MongoDB gespeichert."
                            if enabled else "Das Archiv wurde deaktiviert."),
                           COLOR_SUCCESS if enabled else COLOR_WARNING), ephemeral=True)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "setarchive", "message_archive", f"Enabled: {enabled}")


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# PERMISSIONS-AUDITOR
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
@bot.tree.command(name="audit-perms", description="Prüft alle Rollen auf gefährliche Berechtigungen & Hierarchie")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_audit_perms(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    await interaction.response.defer(ephemeral=True, thinking=True)
    guild = interaction.guild
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(guild.id)
    audit_cfg = cfg.get("perms_audit", {}) or {}
    danger_perms: List[str] = audit_cfg.get("danger_perms", [
        "administrator", "manage_guild", "manage_roles", "manage_channels",
        "ban_members", "kick_members", "mention_everyone",
        "manage_webhooks", "manage_messages", "moderate_members",
    ])
    max_safe_pct = int(audit_cfg.get("max_safe_position_pct", 80))
    findings: List[Tuple[str, str, str]] = []
    total_roles = max(len(guild.roles) - 1, 1)
    for role in sorted(guild.roles, key=lambda r: r.position, reverse=True):
        if role.is_default():
            perms = role.permissions
            risky = [p for p in danger_perms if getattr(perms, p, False)]
            if risky:
                findings.append(("CRITICAL", "@everyone", f"@everyone hat **{', '.join(risky)}** – sofort entfernen!"))
            continue
        perms = role.permissions
        risky = [p for p in danger_perms if getattr(perms, p, False)]
        member_count = len(role.members)
        position_pct = int((role.position / total_roles) * 100)
        if perms.administrator:
            extra = f" – aber **{member_count} Member**!" if member_count > 5 else ""
            findings.append(("CRITICAL", role.name,
                              f"`Administrator` aktiv{extra}. Position: #{role.position} ({position_pct}%). Member: {member_count}."))
            continue
        if risky:
            sev = "HIGH" if any(p in risky for p in ("ban_members", "manage_guild", "manage_roles", "manage_webhooks")) else "MEDIUM"
            note = ""
            if "mention_everyone" in risky and member_count > 20:
                note = f" ⚠️ {member_count} Member können @everyone pingen!"
            if position_pct > max_safe_pct:
                note += f" ⚠️ Sehr hohe Hierarchie-Position ({position_pct}%)."
            findings.append((sev, role.name,
                              f"Gefährliche Perms: **{', '.join(risky)}**. Position #{role.position} ({position_pct}%). Member: {member_count}.{note}"))
    bot_member = guild.me
    bot_top = bot_member.top_role
    higher_roles = [r for r in guild.roles if r.position > bot_top.position and not r.is_default()]
    if higher_roles:
        findings.append(("HIGH", "Bot-Hierarchie",
                          f"Bot-Top-Rolle ist **{bot_top.name}** (#{bot_top.position}). "
                          f"**{len(higher_roles)} Rolle(n) darüber** – diese kann ModForge **nicht moderieren**: "
                          f"{', '.join(r.name for r in higher_roles[:5])}" + (" …" if len(higher_roles) > 5 else "")))
    if guild.mfa_level == discord.MFALevel.disabled:
        findings.append(("MEDIUM", "Server-Settings", "**2FA-Pflicht für Mods ist DEAKTIVIERT**"))
    if guild.verification_level.value < 2:
        findings.append(("LOW", "Server-Settings",
                          f"Verifizierungs-Level ist **{guild.verification_level.name}** – empfohlen: MEDIUM oder höher."))
    sev_color = {"CRITICAL": COLOR_DANGER, "HIGH": COLOR_DANGER, "MEDIUM": COLOR_WARNING, "LOW": COLOR_INFO}
    sev_emoji = {"CRITICAL": "🔴", "HIGH": "🟠", "MEDIUM": "🟡", "LOW": "🔵"}
    if not findings:
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.SHIELD} Permissions-Audit – {guild.name}",
                             f"{E.OK} Keine Auffälligkeiten.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
        await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)
        return
    severity_order = {"CRITICAL": 0, "HIGH": 1, "MEDIUM": 2, "LOW": 3}
    findings.sort(key=lambda f: severity_order.get(f[0], 9))
    worst = findings[0][0]
    desc_lines = [f"{sev_emoji.get(sev, '⚪')} **[{sev}] {label}**\n{msg}" for sev, label, msg in findings[:25]]
    if len(findings) > 25:
        desc_lines.append(f"\n_…und {len(findings) - 25} weitere Funde._")
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.SHIELD} Permissions-Audit – {guild.name}",
                         "\n\n".join(desc_lines)[:4000], sev_color.get(worst, COLOR_WARNING))
    embed.set_footer(text=f"{len(findings)} Befunde · ModForge Security Audit")
    await bot.log_action(guild, f"{E.SHIELD} Permissions-Audit ausgeführt",
                         f"**Von:** {interaction.user.mention}\n**Befunde:** {len(findings)} (höchste Stufe: {worst})",
                         sev_color.get(worst, COLOR_WARNING), user=interaction.user, module="audit")
    ACTIVITY.push("audit", f"Audit auf {guild.name} – {len(findings)} Befunde (worst: {worst}).",
                  guild_id=guild.id, guild_name=guild.name)
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)

    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, view=view)

@bot.tree.command(name="logs", description="Setzt den Standard-Log-Kanal")

@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)

    cfg["log_channel"] = channel.id
    await bot.db.set_config(interaction.guild.id, cfg)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.CHANNEL} Standard-Log-Kanal gesetzt",
                         f"Standard-Log-Kanal auf {channel.mention} gesetzt.\n"
