    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "logs_set", "logging", f"Kanal: {channel.id}")


def _module_choices() -> List[app_commands.Choice[str]]:
    return [app_commands.Choice(name=m, value=m) for m in LOG_MODULES[:25]]


@bot.tree.command(name="logset", description="Setzt den Log-Kanal für ein bestimmtes Modul")
@app_commands.describe(module="Modul wählen", channel="Kanal für dieses Modul")
@app_commands.choices(module=_module_choices())
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_logset(interaction: discord.Interaction, module: app_commands.Choice[str],
                       channel: discord.TextChannel) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    log_channels = cfg.get("log_channels", {}) or {}
    log_channels[module.value] = channel.id
    cfg["log_channels"] = log_channels
    await bot.db.set_config(interaction.guild.id, cfg)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Modul-Log-Kanal gesetzt",
                         f"Modul **{module.value}** loggt jetzt in {channel.mention}.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "logset", module.value, f"Kanal: {channel.id}")


@bot.tree.command(name="logreset", description="Setzt den Log-Kanal für ein Modul zurück")
@app_commands.describe(module="Modul wählen")
@app_commands.choices(module=_module_choices())
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_logreset(interaction: discord.Interaction, module: app_commands.Choice[str]) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    log_channels = cfg.get("log_channels", {}) or {}
    log_channels.pop(module.value, None)
    cfg["log_channels"] = log_channels
    await bot.db.set_config(interaction.guild.id, cfg)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Modul-Log zurückgesetzt",
                         f"**{module.value}** nutzt jetzt wieder den Standard-Log-Kanal.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@bot.tree.command(name="logview", description="Zeigt alle konfigurierten Log-Kanäle")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_logview(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    default_id = cfg.get("log_channel")
    log_channels = cfg.get("log_channels", {}) or {}
    fields = [("Standard / Fallback", f"<#{default_id}>" if default_id else "*Nicht gesetzt*", False)]
    for mod in LOG_MODULES[:20]:
        cid = log_channels.get(mod)
        fields.append((mod, f"<#{cid}>" if cid else "*Standard*", True))
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.CHANNEL} Log-Konfiguration", "Übersicht aller Log-Kanäle pro Modul.", COLOR_INFO, fields)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)


@bot.tree.command(name="logmodules", description="Listet alle verfügbaren Log-Module")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_logmodules(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    text = "\n".join(f"• `{m}`" for m in LOG_MODULES)
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.CHANNEL} Verfügbare Log-Module", text, COLOR_INFO)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)

@bot.tree.command(name="security_level", description="Setzt die Sicherheitsstufe des Servers")
@app_commands.describe(level="Stufe 0-3")
@app_commands.choices(level=[
    app_commands.Choice(name="Level 0: Normal", value=0),
    app_commands.Choice(name="Level 1: Erhöht", value=1),
    app_commands.Choice(name="Level 2: Sturmflut (Auto-Kick neue Accounts)", value=2),
    app_commands.Choice(name="Level 3: BLACKOUT (Server eingefroren)", value=3)
])
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_security_level(interaction: discord.Interaction, level: app_commands.Choice[int]) -> None:
    cfg = bot.db.get_config(interaction.guild.id)
    cfg["security_level"] = level.value
    await bot.db.set_config(interaction.guild.id, cfg)
    if level.value == 3:
        await _activate_lockdown(interaction.guild)
        bot.tracker.lockdown_active[interaction.guild.id] = True
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.SHIELD} Sicherheitsstufe geändert",
                         f"Der Server befindet sich nun auf **{level.name}**.",
                         COLOR_DANGER if level.value > 0 else COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed)
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "security_level", "security", f"Level: {level.value}")

    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed)

                                   "unlockdown", "security", "Lockdown aufgehoben")


@bot.tree.command(name="massunban", description="Entbannt alle gebannten Nutzer (Rate-Limit-geschützt)")
@app_commands.default_permissions(administrator=True)
async def slash_massunban(interaction: discord.Interaction) -> None:
    await interaction.response.defer()
    bans = [entry async for entry in interaction.guild.bans()]
    count = 0
    for ban_entry in bans:
        try:
            await rate_limited(
                lambda be=ban_entry: interaction.guild.unban(be.user, reason=f"Mass-Unban durch {interaction.user}")
            )
            count += 1
        except (discord.Forbidden, discord.NotFound):
            pass
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.OK} Mass-Unban abgeschlossen",
                         f"**{count}** von {len(bans)} Nutzern wurden entbannt.", COLOR_SUCCESS)
    await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed)
    await bot.log_action(interaction.guild, f"{E.OK} Mass-Unban",
                         f"{interaction.user.mention} hat {count} Nutzer entbannt.",
                         COLOR_SUCCESS, module="moderation")
    await bot.db.aadd_admin_audit(interaction.guild.id, interaction.user.id, str(interaction.user),
                                   "massunban", "moderation", f"Unbanned: {count}/{len(bans)}")


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# ERROR HANDLING
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
@bot.event
async def on_command_error(ctx: commands.Context, error: Exception) -> None:
    if isinstance(error, commands.MissingPermissions):
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Keine Berechtigung",
                             "Du hast keine Berechtigung für diesen Command.", COLOR_DANGER)
        await ctx.send(embed=embed)
    elif isinstance(error, commands.MemberNotFound):
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Nutzer nicht gefunden",
                             "Der angegebene Nutzer wurde nicht gefunden.", COLOR_DANGER)
        await ctx.send(embed=embed)
    elif isinstance(error, commands.BadArgument):
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Ungültiges Argument", f"Ungültiges Argument: `{error}`", COLOR_DANGER)
        await ctx.send(embed=embed)
    elif isinstance(error, commands.CheckFailure):
        embed = create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Zugriff verweigert",
                             "Du hast keine Berechtigung für diesen Command.", COLOR_DANGER)
        await ctx.send(embed=embed)
    elif isinstance(error, commands.CommandNotFound):
        return
    else:
        log.error(f"Command-Fehler: {error}")


@bot.tree.error
async def on_app_command_error(interaction: discord.Interaction, error: app_commands.AppCommandError) -> None:
    cmd_name = interaction.command.qualified_name if interaction.command else "unbekannt"
    user_msg: Optional[str] = None
    color = COLOR_DANGER
    if isinstance(error, app_commands.CommandOnCooldown):
        user_msg = f"{E.CLOCK} Bitte warte noch **{error.retry_after:.1f}s**."
        color = COLOR_WARNING
    elif isinstance(error, app_commands.MissingPermissions):
        user_msg = f"{E.FAIL} Dir fehlen Berechtigungen: `{', '.join(error.missing_permissions)}`"
    elif isinstance(error, app_commands.BotMissingPermissions):
        user_msg = f"{E.FAIL} Dem Bot fehlen Berechtigungen: `{', '.join(error.missing_permissions)}`"
    elif isinstance(error, app_commands.CheckFailure):
        user_msg = f"{E.FAIL} Du hast keinen Zugriff auf diesen Befehl."
    elif isinstance(error, app_commands.CommandNotFound):
        user_msg = f"{E.FAIL} Befehl nicht (mehr) verfügbar."
    elif isinstance(error, app_commands.TransformerError):
        user_msg = f"{E.FAIL} Ungültiger Parameterwert."
    embed = create_embed(f"{E.FAIL} Fehler",
                         user_msg or f"Ein unerwarteter Fehler ist aufgetreten: `{str(error)[:200]}`", color)
    try:
        if interaction.response.is_done():
            await interaction.followup.send(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)
        else:
            await interaction.response.send_message(embed=embed, ephemeral=True)
    except (discord.HTTPException, discord.NotFound):
        pass
    if user_msg is not None:
        log.warning(f"Slash-Cmd '{cmd_name}' von {interaction.user}: {type(error).__name__}: {error}")
        return
    original = getattr(error, "original", error)
    tb = "".join(traceback.format_exception(type(original), original, original.__traceback__))
    log.error(f"Unhandled Slash-Cmd-Fehler in '{cmd_name}' (User {interaction.user}, Guild {interaction.guild_id}):\n{tb}")
    if interaction.guild:
        snippet = tb[-1500:] if len(tb) > 1500 else tb
        await bot.log_action(
            interaction.guild, f"{E.FAIL} Slash-Command Exception",
            f"**Befehl:** `/{cmd_name}`\n**Nutzer:** {interaction.user.mention} (`{interaction.user.id}`)\n"
            f"**Typ:** `{type(original).__name__}`\n```py\n{snippet}\n```",
            COLOR_DANGER, user=interaction.user if isinstance(interaction.user, discord.Member) else None, module="errors",
        )


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# WEB-FRONTEND (Landing Page · Status · Admin · OAuth2 · Dashboard)
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
app = Flask("modforge_web")
app.secret_key = os.getenv("SESSION_SECRET") or secrets_mod.token_hex(32)
app.config["PERMANENT_SESSION_LIFETIME"] = 60 * 60 * 4

from werkzeug.middleware.proxy_fix import ProxyFix

app.wsgi_app = ProxyFix(
    app.wsgi_app,
    x_proto=1,         # X-Forwarded-Proto
    x_host=1,          # X-Forwarded-Host
    x_port=1,          # X-Forwarded-Port (optional)
    x_prefix=1         # X-Forwarded-Prefix (optional)
)

# Session-Cookie sicher konfigurieren
app.config.update(
    SESSION_COOKIE_SECURE=True,    # Nur über HTTPS senden
    SESSION_COOKIE_SAMESITE='Lax',  # Erlaubt Redirects von Discord
    SESSION_COOKIE_HTTPONLY=True    # Kein JavaScript-Zugriff
)

ADMIN_PASSWORD = os.getenv("ADMIN_PASSWORD", "").strip()
ADMIN_USERNAME = os.getenv("ADMIN_USERNAME", "admin").strip() or "admin"

_LOGIN_ATTEMPTS: Dict[str, deque] = defaultdict(deque)
_LOGIN_LOCK = threading.Lock()
LOGIN_WINDOW = 300
LOGIN_MAX_TRIES = 7

DISCORD_PERMISSIONS_ADMIN = 8  # Administrator flag


def _client_ip() -> str:
    return (request.headers.get("X-Forwarded-For", request.remote_addr or "?")).split(",")[0].strip()


def _rate_limited_web(ip: str) -> bool:
    now = time.time()
    with _LOGIN_LOCK:
        dq = _LOGIN_ATTEMPTS[ip]
        while dq and now - dq[0] > LOGIN_WINDOW:
            dq.popleft()
        return len(dq) >= LOGIN_MAX_TRIES


def _record_attempt(ip: str) -> None:
    with _LOGIN_LOCK:
        _LOGIN_ATTEMPTS[ip].append(time.time())


def _run_async(coro, timeout: float = 8.0):
    if BOT_REF is None or not BOT_REF.loop or not BOT_REF.loop.is_running():
        return None
    try:
        fut = asyncio.run_coroutine_threadsafe(coro, BOT_REF.loop)
        return fut.result(timeout=timeout)
    except Exception as ex:
        log.debug(f"_run_async Fehler: {ex}")
        return None


def admin_required(fn: Callable) -> Callable:
    @wraps(fn)
    def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
        if not session.get("admin"):
            return redirect(url_for("admin_login"))
        return fn(*args, **kwargs)
    return wrapper


def dashboard_login_required(fn: Callable) -> Callable:
    """Schützt Dashboard-Routen mit Discord OAuth2-Session."""
    @wraps(fn)
    def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
        if not session.get("discord_user"):
            return redirect(url_for("auth_discord"))
        return fn(*args, **kwargs)
    return wrapper


def _discord_api_get(endpoint: str, access_token: str) -> Optional[dict]:
    if not _REQUESTS_AVAILABLE:
        return None
    try:
        resp = _requests.get(
            f"{DISCORD_API_BASE}/{endpoint}",
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {access_token}"},
            timeout=10
        )
        if resp.status_code == 200:
            return resp.json()
    except Exception as e:
        log.debug(f"Discord API error: {e}")
    return None

    <details>
        <summary>Ist ModForge kostenlos?</summary>
        <div class="content">Ja! ModForge ist vollständig kostenlos nutzbar. Alle Features sind inklusive.</div>
    </details>
    <details>
        <summary>Wie konfiguriere ich den Bot?</summary>
        <div class="content">Nutze das Web-Dashboard (Login mit Discord) oder die Slash-Commands direkt auf deinem Server. Alle Module sind einzeln konfigurierbar.</div>
    </details>
    <details>
        <summary>Wie funktioniert das Backup-System?</summary>
        <div class="content">Mit <code>/backup create</code> erstellst du einen vollständigen Snapshot deines Servers (Rollen, Kanäle, Farben, Rechte). Du erhältst eine Backup-ID. Mit <code>/backup restore &lt;id&gt;</code> kannst du das Backup auch auf einem anderen Server wiederherstellen.</div>
    </details>
    <details>
        <summary>Wie lösche ich meine Daten (DSGVO)?</summary>
        <div class="content">Schreibe dem Bot eine DM mit <code>!dsgvo</code> oder nutze den Slash-Command <code>/gdpr</code> auf einem Server. Deine Daten werden vollständig gelöscht, Cases werden anonymisiert.</div>
    </details>
    <details>
        <summary>Was ist das Geo/VPN-Gate?</summary>
        <div class="content">Wenn aktiviert, erkennt das Verifizierungssystem bekannte Hosting/VPN-IPs und fordert eine manuelle Freigabe durch einen Moderator an, bevor der Nutzer verifiziert wird.</div>
    </details>

<script>
function fmtUptime(s){
    s=Math.floor(s); var d=Math.floor(s/86400);s%=86400; var h=Math.floor(s/3600);s%=3600; var m=Math.floor(s/60);
    return (d?d+'d ':'')+( h?h+'h ':'')+m+'m';
}
function escapeHtml(s){ return (s||'').replace(/[&<>"']/g,function(c){return{'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c];}); }
async function tick(){
    try{
        var r=await fetch('/admin/api/state'); if(!r.ok)return; var d=await r.json();
        document.getElementById('k-guilds').textContent=d.stats.guild_count;
        document.getElementById('k-members').textContent=d.stats.member_total.toLocaleString('de-DE');
        document.getElementById('k-uptime').textContent=fmtUptime(d.stats.uptime_s);
        document.getElementById('k-latency').textContent=d.stats.latency_ms;
        document.getElementById('k-cases').textContent=d.stats.cases_total;
        document.getElementById('k-archive').textContent=d.stats.archive_total;
        var tg=document.querySelector('#t-guilds tbody');
        tg.innerHTML=d.guilds.map(function(g){return'<tr><td>'+escapeHtml(g.name)+'</td><td><span class="tag">'+g.id+'</span></td><td>'+(g.member_count||0).toLocaleString('de-DE')+'</td><td>'+escapeHtml(g.owner||'?')+'</td><td class="muted">'+(g.created||'')+'</td><td><a href="/guild/'+g.id+'/dashboard" class="btn small">Config</a></td></tr>';}).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="6" style="color:var(--muted)">Keine Server.</td></tr>';
        var eg=document.getElementById('ev-guilds');
        eg.innerHTML=d.guild_events.map(function(e){return'<div class="evt"><span class="kind '+(e.event==="join"?"guild_join":"guild_leave")+'">'+e.event+'</span><b>'+escapeHtml(e.guild_name)+'</b> &ndash; '+(e.member_count||'?')+' Member<div class="ts">'+e.timestamp+'</div></div>';}).join('')||'<div class="evt" style="color:var(--muted)">Keine Events.</div>';
        var ea=document.getElementById('ev-activity');
        ea.innerHTML=d.activity.map(function(a){return'<div class="evt"><span class="kind '+escapeHtml(a.kind)+'">'+escapeHtml(a.kind)+'</span>'+escapeHtml(a.text)+'<div class="ts">'+a.ts+'</div></div>';}).join('')||'<div class="evt" style="color:var(--muted)">Stream leer.</div>';
        var tm=document.querySelector('#t-msgs tbody');
        tm.innerHTML=d.recent_messages.map(function(m){return'<tr><td style="color:var(--muted)">'+m.timestamp+'</td><td><span class="tag">'+m.guild_id+'</span></td><td><span class="tag">'+m.user_id+'</span></td><td><span class="tag">'+m.channel_id+'</span></td><td>'+escapeHtml((m.content||'').slice(0,200))+(m.deleted?'<span class="tag err">deleted</span>':'')+'</td></tr>';}).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="5" style="color:var(--muted)">Archiv leer.</td></tr>';
        var tc=document.querySelector('#t-cases tbody');
        tc.innerHTML=d.recent_cases.map(function(c){return'<tr><td><b>#'+c.case_id+'</b></td><td><span class="tag">'+c.guild_id+'</span></td><td><span class="tag">'+c.user_id+'</span></td><td><span class="tag '+(c.action==="ban"?"err":c.action==="kick"?"warn":"ok")+'">'+c.action+'</span></td><td>'+escapeHtml((c.reason||'').slice(0,160))+'</td><td style="color:var(--muted)">'+c.created_at+'</td></tr>';}).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="6" style="color:var(--muted)">Keine Cases.</td></tr>';
    }catch(e){console.error(e);}
}
tick(); setInterval(tick,5000);
</script>
</body></html>"""

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# FLASK ROUTES
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
@app.route("/")
def home_page() -> str:
    client_id = ""
    guild_count = 0
    member_total = 0
    uptime_s = 0
    latency_ms = 0
    try:
        if BOT_REF and BOT_REF.user:
            client_id = str(BOT_REF.user.id)
        if BOT_REF:
            guild_count = len(BOT_REF.guilds)
            member_total = sum(g.member_count or 0 for g in BOT_REF.guilds)
            uptime_s = get_uptime(BOT_REF.start_time)
            latency_ms = round(BOT_REF.latency * 1000, 1)
    except Exception:
        pass
    return render_template_string(LANDING_HTML, client_id=client_id, guild_count=guild_count,
                                  member_total=member_total, uptime_s=uptime_s, latency_ms=latency_ms)


@app.route("/status")
def status_page() -> str:
    uptime_s = 0
    latency_ms = 0
    guild_count = 0
    member_total = 0
    try:
        if BOT_REF:
            uptime_s = get_uptime(BOT_REF.start_time)
            latency_ms = round(BOT_REF.latency * 1000, 1)
            guild_count = len(BOT_REF.guilds)
            member_total = sum(g.member_count or 0 for g in BOT_REF.guilds)
    except Exception:
        pass
    return render_template_string(STATUS_HTML, uptime_s=uptime_s, latency_ms=latency_ms,
                                  guild_count=guild_count, member_total=member_total)


@app.route("/changelog")
def changelog_page() -> str:
    return render_template_string(CHANGELOG_HTML, changelog=CHANGELOG)


@app.route("/terms")
def terms_page() -> str:
    return render_template_string(TERMS_HTML, today=datetime.date.today().isoformat())


@app.route("/privacy")
def privacy_page() -> str:
    return render_template_string(PRIVACY_HTML, today=datetime.date.today().isoformat())


@app.route("/imprint")
def imprint_page() -> str:
    return render_template_string(IMPRINT_HTML)


@app.route("/healthz")
def healthz() -> Any:
    return jsonify({
        "ok": True,
        "bot_ready": bool(BOT_REF and BOT_REF.is_ready()),
        "ts": datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
    })


@app.route("/metrics")
def metrics_endpoint():
    uptime_s = 0
    latency_ms = 0
    guild_count = 0
    member_total = 0
    cases_total = 0
    archive_total = 0
    try:
        if BOT_REF:
            uptime_s = get_uptime(BOT_REF.start_time)
            latency_ms = round(BOT_REF.latency * 1000, 1)
            guild_count = len(BOT_REF.guilds)
            member_total = sum(g.member_count or 0 for g in BOT_REF.guilds)
        cases_total = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.cases.count_documents({})) or 0
        archive_total = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.message_archive.count_documents({})) or 0
    except Exception:
        pass
    metrics = (
        f"# HELP modforge_uptime_seconds Bot uptime in seconds\n"
        f"# TYPE modforge_uptime_seconds gauge\n"
        f"modforge_uptime_seconds {uptime_s}\n"
        f"# HELP modforge_latency_ms Discord gateway latency in ms\n"
        f"# TYPE modforge_latency_ms gauge\n"
        f"modforge_latency_ms {latency_ms}\n"
        f"# HELP modforge_guilds Number of guilds\n"
        f"# TYPE modforge_guilds gauge\n"
        f"modforge_guilds {guild_count}\n"
        f"# HELP modforge_members Total members across guilds\n"
        f"# TYPE modforge_members gauge\n"
        f"modforge_members {member_total}\n"
        f"# HELP modforge_cases Total moderation cases\n"
        f"# TYPE modforge_cases gauge\n"
        f"modforge_cases {cases_total}\n"
        f"# HELP modforge_archive_messages Total archived messages\n"
        f"# TYPE modforge_archive_messages gauge\n"
        f"modforge_archive_messages {archive_total}\n"
    )
    return Response(metrics, mimetype="text/plain; charset=utf-8")


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# ADMIN LOGIN ROUTES
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
@app.route("/admin/login", methods=["GET", "POST"])
def admin_login() -> Any:
    if not ADMIN_PASSWORD:
        return render_template_string(LOGIN_HTML, error="Admin-Login deaktiviert: Setze ADMIN_PASSWORD.")
    error = None
    ip = _client_ip()
    if request.method == "POST":
        if _rate_limited_web(ip):
            error = "Zu viele Versuche."
        else:
            user = (request.form.get("username") or "").strip()
            pw = (request.form.get("password") or "")
            if secrets_mod.compare_digest(user, ADMIN_USERNAME) and secrets_mod.compare_digest(pw, ADMIN_PASSWORD):
                session.permanent = True
                session["admin"] = True
                session["admin_since"] = time.time()
                ACTIVITY.push("admin_login", f"Admin-Login erfolgreich von {ip}.")
                return redirect(url_for("admin_dashboard"))
            else:
                _record_attempt(ip)
                ACTIVITY.push("admin_login_fail", f"Fehlgeschlagener Login von {ip}.")
                error = "Falsche Zugangsdaten."
    return render_template_string(LOGIN_HTML, error=error)


@app.route("/admin/logout")
def admin_logout() -> Any:
    session.pop("admin", None)
    return redirect(url_for("admin_login"))


@app.route("/admin/dashboard")
@admin_required
def admin_dashboard() -> str:
    return render_template_string(DASHBOARD_HTML)


@app.route("/admin/api/state")
@admin_required
def admin_api_state() -> Any:
    if BOT_REF is None:
        return jsonify({"stats": {}, "guilds": [], "guild_events": [], "activity": [], "recent_messages": [], "recent_cases": []})
    guilds_payload = []
    member_total = 0
    for g in list(BOT_REF.guilds):
        member_total += g.member_count or 0
        guilds_payload.append({
            "id": g.id, "name": g.name, "member_count": g.member_count or 0,
            "owner": str(g.owner) if g.owner else str(g.owner_id),
            "created": g.created_at.strftime("%Y-%m-%d") if g.created_at else "",
        })
    guilds_payload.sort(key=lambda x: x["member_count"], reverse=True)
    latency_ms = int((BOT_REF.latency or 0) * 1000)
    uptime_s = get_uptime(BOT_REF.start_time)
    cases_total = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.cases.count_documents({})) or 0
    archive_total = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.message_archive.count_documents({})) or 0
    recent_cases_raw = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.cases.find({}).sort("created_at", -1).limit(20).to_list(20)) or []
    recent_cases = [{
        "case_id": c.get("case_id"), "guild_id": c.get("guild_id"), "user_id": c.get("user_id"),
        "action": c.get("action"), "reason": c.get("reason", "")[:160],
        "created_at": c["created_at"].strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S") if c.get("created_at") else "",
    } for c in recent_cases_raw]
    recent_msgs_raw = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.message_archive.find({}).sort("timestamp", -1).limit(25).to_list(25)) or []
    recent_messages = [{
        "guild_id": m.get("guild_id"), "channel_id": m.get("channel_id"), "user_id": m.get("user_id"),
        "content": m.get("content", ""), "deleted": bool(m.get("deleted")),
        "timestamp": m["timestamp"].strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S") if m.get("timestamp") else "",
    } for m in recent_msgs_raw]
    guild_events_raw = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.aget_recent_guild_events(limit=30)) or []
    guild_events = [{
        "guild_name": e.get("guild_name", "?"), "event": e.get("event"),
        "member_count": e.get("member_count", "?"),
        "timestamp": e["timestamp"].strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S") if e.get("timestamp") else "",
    } for e in guild_events_raw]
    return jsonify({
        "stats": {"guild_count": len(guilds_payload), "member_total": member_total,
                  "uptime_s": uptime_s, "latency_ms": latency_ms,
                  "cases_total": cases_total, "archive_total": archive_total},
        "guilds": guilds_payload[:50], "guild_events": guild_events,
        "activity": ACTIVITY.snapshot(limit=80),
        "recent_messages": recent_messages, "recent_cases": recent_cases,
    })


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# DISCORD OAUTH2 DASHBOARD ROUTES
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
@app.route("/dashboard")
def dashboard_index() -> Any:
    if not session.get("discord_user"):
        if not DISCORD_CLIENT_ID or not DISCORD_CLIENT_SECRET:
            return render_template_string(DISCORD_LOGIN_HTML, client_id="",
                                          oauth_url="#", error="Dashboard nicht konfiguriert (OAuth2-Keys fehlen).")
        state = secrets_mod.token_urlsafe(16)
        session["oauth_state"] = state
        oauth_url = (
            f"https://discord.com/api/oauth2/authorize"
            f"?client_id={DISCORD_CLIENT_ID}"
            f"&redirect_uri={DISCORD_REDIRECT_URI}"
            f"&response_type=code"
            f"&scope={DISCORD_OAUTH_SCOPES.replace(' ', '%20')}"
            f"&state={state}"
        )
        return render_template_string(DISCORD_LOGIN_HTML, client_id=DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
                                      oauth_url=oauth_url, error=None)
    # Eingeloggt: Server-Liste zeigen
    user = session["discord_user"]
    guilds = session.get("discord_guilds", [])
    # Nur Server mit Admin-Permission oder wo Bot aktiv ist
    admin_guilds = []
    bot_guild_ids = set()
    if BOT_REF:
        bot_guild_ids = {str(g.id) for g in BOT_REF.guilds}
    for g in guilds:
        permissions = int(g.get("permissions", 0))
        is_admin = bool(permissions & DISCORD_PERMISSIONS_ADMIN)
        if is_admin:
            g["has_bot"] = g["id"] in bot_guild_ids
            if BOT_REF:
                bot_guild = BOT_REF.get_guild(int(g["id"])) if g["id"].isdigit() else None
                if bot_guild:
                    g["member_count"] = bot_guild.member_count
            admin_guilds.append(g)
    return render_template_string(GUILD_SELECT_HTML, user=user, guilds=admin_guilds)


@app.route("/auth/discord")
def auth_discord() -> Any:
    if not DISCORD_CLIENT_ID or not DISCORD_CLIENT_SECRET:
        return redirect(url_for("dashboard_index"))
    state = secrets_mod.token_urlsafe(16)
    session["oauth_state"] = state
    oauth_url = (
        f"https://discord.com/api/oauth2/authorize"
        f"?client_id={DISCORD_CLIENT_ID}"
        f"&redirect_uri={DISCORD_REDIRECT_URI}"
        f"&response_type=code"
        f"&scope={DISCORD_OAUTH_SCOPES.replace(' ', '%20')}"
        f"&state={state}"
    )
    return redirect(oauth_url)


@app.route("/auth/callback")
def auth_callback() -> Any:
    code = request.args.get("code")
    state = request.args.get("state")
    if not code:
        return redirect(url_for("dashboard_index"))
    if state != session.get("oauth_state"):
        return render_template_string(DISCORD_LOGIN_HTML, client_id=DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
                                      oauth_url="#", error="Ungültiger OAuth2-State. Versuche es erneut.")
    if not _REQUESTS_AVAILABLE:
        return render_template_string(DISCORD_LOGIN_HTML, client_id=DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
                                      oauth_url="#", error="requests-Bibliothek nicht installiert.")
    try:
        token_resp = _requests.post(
            f"{DISCORD_API_BASE}/oauth2/token",
            data={
                "client_id": DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
                "client_secret": DISCORD_CLIENT_SECRET,
                "grant_type": "authorization_code",
                "code": code,
                "redirect_uri": DISCORD_REDIRECT_URI,
            },
            headers={"Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"},
            timeout=10
        )
        if token_resp.status_code != 200:
            return render_template_string(DISCORD_LOGIN_HTML, client_id=DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
                                          oauth_url="#", error=f"Token-Fehler: {token_resp.status_code}")
        token_data = token_resp.json()
        access_token = token_data.get("access_token")
        if not access_token:
            return render_template_string(DISCORD_LOGIN_HTML, client_id=DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
                                          oauth_url="#", error="Kein Access-Token erhalten.")
        user_data = _discord_api_get("users/@me", access_token)
        guilds_data = _discord_api_get("users/@me/guilds", access_token) or []
        if not user_data:
            return render_template_string(DISCORD_LOGIN_HTML, client_id=DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
                                          oauth_url="#", error="Nutzer-Daten konnten nicht abgerufen werden.")
        session.permanent = True
        session["discord_user"] = {
            "id": user_data.get("id"),
            "username": user_data.get("username"),
            "discriminator": user_data.get("discriminator", "0"),
            "avatar": user_data.get("avatar"),
        }
        session["discord_guilds"] = guilds_data
        session.pop("oauth_state", None)
        ACTIVITY.push("dashboard_login", f"Dashboard-Login: {user_data.get('username', '?')}")
        return redirect(url_for("dashboard_index"))
    except Exception as e:
        log.error(f"OAuth2-Callback Fehler: {e}")
        return render_template_string(DISCORD_LOGIN_HTML, client_id=DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
                                      oauth_url="#", error=f"Fehler beim Login: {e}")


@app.route("/dashboard/logout")
def dashboard_logout() -> Any:
    session.pop("discord_user", None)
    session.pop("discord_guilds", None)
    return redirect(url_for("dashboard_index"))


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# GUILD CONFIG DASHBOARD
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
def _check_guild_access(guild_id: str) -> bool:
    """Prüft ob der eingeloggte Discord-Nutzer Admin auf diesem Server ist."""
    guilds = session.get("discord_guilds", [])
    for g in guilds:
        if g["id"] == guild_id:
            permissions = int(g.get("permissions", 0))
            return bool(permissions & DISCORD_PERMISSIONS_ADMIN)
    return False


@app.route("/guild/<guild_id>/dashboard", methods=["GET", "POST"])
@dashboard_login_required
def guild_dashboard(guild_id: str) -> Any:
    if not _check_guild_access(guild_id):
        return render_template_string(DISCORD_LOGIN_HTML, client_id=DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
                                      oauth_url="#", error="Du hast keinen Admin-Zugriff auf diesen Server.")
    guild_name = "Unbekannt"
    guild_icon = None
    msg = None
    msg_type = "success"
    try:
        gid = int(guild_id)
    except ValueError:
        return "Ungültige Guild-ID", 400

    if BOT_REF:
        bot_guild = BOT_REF.get_guild(gid)
        if bot_guild:
            guild_name = bot_guild.name
            guild_icon = str(bot_guild.icon.url) if bot_guild.icon else None

    cfg = None
    if BOT_REF:
        cfg = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.aget_config(gid))
    if cfg is None:
        cfg = DEFAULT_CONFIG.copy()

    if request.method == "POST":
        # Formular-Daten verarbeiten und Config aktualisieren
        form = request.form
        new_cfg = dict(cfg)
        module_keys = [k for k in DEFAULT_CONFIG.keys()
                       if isinstance(DEFAULT_CONFIG[k], dict) and k not in ("log_channels", "perms_audit")]
        for module_key in module_keys:
            if module_key not in new_cfg or not isinstance(new_cfg[module_key], dict):
                new_cfg[module_key] = {}
            # enabled-Checkbox
            enabled_key = f"{module_key}__enabled"
            if enabled_key in form or f"{module_key}__" in "".join(form.keys()):
                new_cfg[module_key]["enabled"] = enabled_key in form
            # Alle anderen Felder
            prefix = f"{module_key}__"
            for form_key, form_val in form.items():
                if form_key.startswith(prefix) and form_key != enabled_key:
                    field_name = form_key[len(prefix):]
                    orig_val = cfg.get(module_key, {}).get(field_name)
                    if isinstance(orig_val, bool):
                        new_cfg[module_key][field_name] = form_val.lower() in ("on", "true", "1", "yes")
                    elif isinstance(orig_val, int):
                        try:
                            new_cfg[module_key][field_name] = int(form_val)
                        except ValueError:
                            pass
                    elif isinstance(orig_val, list):
                        if form_val.strip():
                            items = [i.strip() for i in re.split(r'[,\n]+', form_val) if i.strip()]
                            try:
                                new_cfg[module_key][field_name] = [int(i) if i.isdigit() else i for i in items]
                            except Exception:
                                new_cfg[module_key][field_name] = items
                        else:
                            new_cfg[module_key][field_name] = []
                    else:
                        new_cfg[module_key][field_name] = form_val
        if BOT_REF:
            ok = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.set_config(gid, new_cfg))
            user = session.get("discord_user", {})
            _run_async(BOT_REF.db.aadd_admin_audit(
                gid, int(user.get("id", 0)), user.get("username", "?"),
                "dashboard_save", "web_dashboard", "Konfiguration über Web-Dashboard gespeichert"
            ))
            msg = "Konfiguration gespeichert!"
            msg_type = "success"
            cfg = new_cfg
        else:
            msg = "Bot nicht verfügbar – Konfiguration konnte nicht gespeichert werden."
            msg_type = "error"

    # Module für Template aufbereiten
    display_modules = {}
    for key in ["anti_spam", "anti_nuke", "anti_raid", "anti_mention", "automod",
                "anti_scam", "anti_url_shortener", "verify_system", "ticket_system",
                "welcome_system", "auto_role", "voice_mod", "warn_system", "backup_system"]:
        if key in cfg:
            display_modules[key] = cfg[key]

    return render_template_string(
        GUILD_DASHBOARD_HTML,
        guild_name=guild_name,
        guild_icon=guild_icon,
        guild_id=guild_id,
        modules=display_modules,
        msg=msg,
        msg_type=msg_type,
    )


@app.route("/guild/<guild_id>/api/config", methods=["GET"])
@dashboard_login_required
def guild_api_config(guild_id: str) -> Any:
    if not _check_guild_access(guild_id):
        return jsonify({"error": "Kein Zugriff"}), 403
    try:
        gid = int(guild_id)
    except ValueError:
        return jsonify({"error": "Ungültige ID"}), 400
    if BOT_REF is None:
        return jsonify({"error": "Bot nicht verfügbar"}), 503
    cfg = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.aget_config(gid))
    if cfg is None:
        return jsonify({"error": "Config nicht gefunden"}), 404
    # Sensible Felder ausblenden
    safe_cfg = {k: v for k, v in cfg.items() if k != "_id"}
    return jsonify(safe_cfg)


@app.route("/guild/<guild_id>/api/module/<module>", methods=["POST"])
@dashboard_login_required
def guild_api_module(guild_id: str, module: str) -> Any:
    if not _check_guild_access(guild_id):
        return jsonify({"error": "Kein Zugriff"}), 403
    try:
        gid = int(guild_id)
    except ValueError:
        return jsonify({"error": "Ungültige ID"}), 400
    if BOT_REF is None:
        return jsonify({"error": "Bot nicht verfügbar"}), 503
    data = request.get_json()
    if not data:
        return jsonify({"error": "Kein JSON-Body"}), 400
    cfg = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.aget_config(gid))
    if cfg is None:
        return jsonify({"error": "Config nicht gefunden"}), 404
    if module in cfg and isinstance(cfg[module], dict):
        for key, value in data.items():
            cfg[module][key] = value
        _run_async(BOT_REF.db.set_config(gid, cfg))
        user = session.get("discord_user", {})
        _run_async(BOT_REF.db.aadd_admin_audit(
            gid, int(user.get("id", 0)), user.get("username", "?"),
            f"api_module_{module}", module, f"API-Update: {list(data.keys())}"
        ))
        return jsonify({"ok": True, "module": module})
    return jsonify({"error": f"Modul '{module}' nicht gefunden"}), 404


@app.route("/guild/<guild_id>/api/backups")
@dashboard_login_required
def guild_api_backups(guild_id: str) -> Any:
    if not _check_guild_access(guild_id):
        return jsonify({"error": "Kein Zugriff"}), 403
    try:
        gid = int(guild_id)
    except ValueError:
        return jsonify({"error": "Ungültige ID"}), 400
    if BOT_REF is None:
        return jsonify({"backups": []}), 200
    backups = _run_async(BOT_REF.db.aget_guild_backups(gid)) or []
    result = []
    for b in backups:
        created = b.get("created_at")
        data = b.get("data", {})
        result.append({
            "backup_id": b.get("backup_id"),
            "label": data.get("label", "Automatisch"),
            "created_at": created.isoformat() if isinstance(created, datetime.datetime) else str(created),
            "roles": len(data.get("roles", [])),
            "text_channels": len(data.get("text_channels", [])),
            "voice_channels": len(data.get("voice_channels", [])),
        })
    return jsonify({"backups": result})


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# BOT SERVER STARTUP
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
def run() -> None:
    port = int(os.getenv("PORT", "7860"))
    app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port=port, debug=False, threaded=True)


def keep_alive() -> None:
    threading.Thread(target=run, daemon=True).start()


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# START
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
if __name__ == "__main__":
    keep_alive()
    if BOT_TOKEN == "DEIN_BOT_TOKEN_HIER":
        print("❌ BITTE TOKEN EINTRAGEN! Setze DISCORD_TOKEN als Umgebungsvariable.")
    else:
        bot.run(BOT_TOKEN)
